Thanks to the Ryan White CARE Act, over half a million people a year with HIV/AIDS receive vital services. The epidemic isn‚Äôt over ‚Äì but now life-saving medications are available, new infections have plummeted, and science ‚Äì rather than stigma ‚Äì guides medical care.
